Share your projects and opinions at the Gadget Bar, work-shops, and on the beach. Form new friendships, collaborations and endeavors.</p>\n<p><em><br />\n&#8212; Daniel Kraft MD</em></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-321437 noshadow alignnone\" title=\"signature - Daniel Kraft MD - no. 1\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/signature-Daniel-Kraft-MD-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"302\" height=\"106\" /></p>\n<p>Chair | Exponential Medicine<br />\nFaculty Chair for Medicine | Singularity University</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>IMAGE</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; welcome letter &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>Dear readers,</p>\n<p>There&#8217;s a medical revolution happening.  Every year the top venture capitalists, scientists, and entrepreneurs gather at Exponential Medicine by Singularity University to discuss the intersection of exponential tech, health, and vitality. I co-founded this event with my colleague Daniel Kraft  a decade ago.</p>\n<p>Join us this year to learn about the quantified health movement. Where is quantified health heading? A growing array of tech sensors are becoming available:</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">wearables:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Wearable bracelets &#8212; and wrist-based devices &#8212; can go well beyond steps. Some are designed to fit on fingers called ringables &#8212; such as the <a href=\"https://ouraring.com\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\">Oura</a> ring. They measure heart rate + heart rate variability. There&#8217;s an EKG on <a href=\"https://www.apple.com/watch\" target=\"_blank\">Apple Watch</a>. The United States FDA has also cleared <a href=\"https://www.massdevice.com/fda-clears-biobeats-cuffless-bp-wearable\" target=\"_blank\">cuffless blood pressure tech</a> &#8212; such as this device from <a href=\"https://www.biobeat.cloud\" target=\"_blank\">BioBeat</a>.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">insideables:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Beyond the wrist, we can fit health sensors <a href=\"https://www.zdnet.com/article/how-smart-contact-lenses-will-help-keep-an-eye-on-your-health\" target=\"_blank\">into contact lenses</a>. Embedded RFID chips beneath the skin &#8212; read about my own implant <a href=\"https://www.diamandis.com/blog/why-i-implanted-an-rfid-tag-in-my-hand\" target=\"_blank\">here</a> &#8212; have been used to store data  + unlock doors. And we now have <a href=\"https://profusa.com\" target=\"_blank\">Lumee</a> by Profusa &#8212; a subcutaneous chip that can sense various body chemistries.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">breathables:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Quantifying the molecules in your breath can be useful &#8212; currently used as a method to detect disease.  New nano-nose tech is in clinical trials to conduct breath biopsy &#8212; sampling a person&#8217;s breath to detect the molecular content + patterns that can indicate early stages of lung + other cancers, plus a range of metabolic illness. <a href=\"https://www.owlstonemedical.com\" target=\"_blank\">Owlstone Medical</a> is a global leader in breath biopsy. Some breathables can also quantify ketones in the breath to help people with their target metabolic states.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">underwearables:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>As sensors have become more capable, less expensive &#8212; you can now purchase sensors from <a href=\"https://spirehealth.com\" target=\"_blank\">Spire Health</a> for each pair of your underwear that measure: respiratory rate, activity, heart rate, and sleep.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">trainables:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Feedback provides nudges to help behavior modification. The <a href=\"https://www.uprightpose.com\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\">Upright</a> sensor &#8212; worn on your back &#8212; measures your posture. If persistent slouching is detected it buzzes to remind you. Improved posture may lessen back pain in some people.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">invisibles:<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Wearables require synching + charging. But now we&#8217;re entering a time where our health be measured digitally by ubiquitous sensors. Cameras can now pick-up heart rate + respiratory rate &#8212; for example: <a href=\"https://cocooncam.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Cocoon Cam</a> has a baby monitor on the market.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://kepleranalytics.com\" target=\"_blank\">Kepler Analytics</a> is revolutionizing retail with invisible foot traffic sensors using wireless phone detection tech. Engineers at MIT have prototyped a system called <a href=\"http://witrack.csail.mit.edu\" target=\"_blank\">WiTrack</a> that can wirelessly detect human vital signs, movement, and sleep patters of several people in the same room.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\"><em>Making sense of all the data.</em></span></p>\n<p>As millions of people wear devices and billions of data points are collected daily &#8212; we can start to understand the real-world digital measures of health + illness. The wearable heath tracker <a href=\"https://www.fitbit.com\" target=\"_blank\">FitBit</a> has demonstrated this, for example, in a recent <a href=\"https://finance.yahoo.com/news/exclusive-fitbits-150-billion-hours-heart-data-reveals-secrets-human-health-133124215.html\" target=\"_blank\">story</a>:  FitBit&#8217;s 150 billion hours of heart data reveal secrets about health.</p>\n<p>With crowd-sourced studies such as <a href=\"https://verily.com/projects/precision-medicine/project-baseline/\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\">Project Baseline</a> by <a href=\"https://verily.com\" target=\"_blank\">Verily</a> &#8212; you can gain knowledge from your sleep pattern and how it compares to other people. And potentially find new digital bio-markers indicating medical issues.</p>\n<p>While privacy + data ownership issues are significant challenges &#8212;  crowd-sourced insights can improve wellness, lower costs, and democratize access to improved health care globally.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\"><em>Please meet-up with us.</em></span></p>\n<p>I hope you&#8217;ll attend Exponential Medicine where we&#8217;ll be sharing + discussing the future of wearables &#8212; and the impact they&#8217;ll have on heath care at home + hospital, and the opportunities these devices bring for innovative start-ups + business.</p>\n<p>SIGNATURE</p>\n<p>&#8212; <em>Peter Diamandis MD</em></p>\n<p>co-founder | Exponential Medicine<br />\nco-founder | Singularity University</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; notes &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>AI = artificial intelligence<br />\nEKG = electro-cardio-gram<br />\nRFID = radio frequency identification</p>\n<p>FDA = Federal Drug Administration • United States</p>\n<hr />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">[ story file ]</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">story title:</span> event | Exponential Medicine • by Singularity University<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">deck:</span> theme: The future of health + medicine tech<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">folder:</span> events guide</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">[ end of file ]</span></p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 08 Oct 2019 05:00:17 +0000","feedId":11321,"bgimg":"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-blocks-health-care-no.-2.png","linkMd5":"6d8f66bf054342a882691f7a1821ddac","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn13@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-21-593_04cf5e8404e81316.webp","destWidth":5500,"destHeight":3666,"sourceBytes":20386361,"destBytes":100456,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-blocks-health-care-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn13@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-21-593_04cf5e8404e81316.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/Logo-SU-Exponential-Med.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn1@2020_3/2020/08/25/01-22-27-383_9892df1bf81a9ead.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/Singularity-University-H1.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn87@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-31-692_1a63faa0e25801fa.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/signature-Daniel-Kraft-MD-no.-1.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn28@2020_2/2020/08/25/01-22-32-420_bc59e7a73094b854.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318532657},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","title":"report &#124; Data is growing world-wide, and so is the energy needed to power it","link":"https://www.kurzweilai.net/?p=334867","description":"<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-336603 noshadow\" title=\"photo - computer + data center - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-computer-+-data-center-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"1050\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; in this post &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>~ story<br />\n~ report<br />\n~ key points<br />\n~ quote<br />\n~ featurettes<br />\n~ reading</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; story &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>A study by Northwestern Univ. looks at the world-wide growth of data &#8212; and the global energy needed to power it. The research team asks the question: Will we run out of energy to power civilization&#8217;s data-use &#8212; soon or in the future? According to Microsoft, there are billions of devices and data centers processing over 2.5 exa-bytes of data every day.</p>\n<p>The study&#8217;s analysis paints a detailed picture of global energy-use &#8212; as we attempt to keep-up with today&#8217;s increasing demand for data. Filled with computing and networking equipment: data centers are central locations that collect, store, and process data. As the world relies more + more on data-intensive tech, the energy-use of data centers is a heightened worry.</p>\n<p>While data center facilities have been successful &#8212; to-date &#8212; at using energy efficiently enough to track the rising tide of demand &#8212; analysts warn that when these efficiency measures can no longer match-up, an enormous spike of energy need will happen.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; report &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">group:</span> AAAS<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">publication:</span> <em>Science</em><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">report title:</span> re-Calibrating global data center energy-use estimates<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">author:</span> by Northwestern Univ.<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">date:</span> February 2020<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">read</span> | <a href=\"https://science.sciencemag.org/content/367/6481/984\" target=\"_blank\">report</a></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; summary &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>This analysis presents a nuanced picture of global energy-use. Data centers represent the information backbone of an increasingly digitized world.</p>\n<p>Demand for their services has been rising rapidly<em></em>, and data-intensive tech &#8212; like artificial intelligence, smart + connected energy systems, distributed manufacturing systems, and autonomous vehicles &#8212; promise to increase demand further<em></em>. Data centers are energy-intensive &#8212; accounting for 1% of world-wide electricity-use.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-336914 noshadow\" title=\"photo - computer + data cables - no. 3\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-computer-+-data-cables-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"700\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; key points &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><em>The world is using more + more electronic data &#8212; that equals more energy needed to power it:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li>data is information that&#8217;s created, stored, and transmitted across a wide-range of computer equipment</li>\n<li>this electronic equipment includes:</li>\n<li><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">1.</span>  computer warehouses &#8212; called: data centers</li>\n<li><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">2.</span>  satellite + cable systems &#8212; called: tele-communications networks</li>\n<li><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">3.</span>  desktop + mobile computing</li>\n<li><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">4.</span>  smart-devices, smart-accessories, smart-vehicles, smart-home, smart-buildings, smart-city</li>\n<li>these tools: make + hold information • send + receive data</li>\n<li>these tools: require enormous energy (electricity) to function</li>\n<li>especially data centers &#8212; the computers inside need constant refrigeration</li>\n<li>refrigeration cools computer equipment to protect it from over-heating + failing</li>\n<li>data centers use high amounts of energy for all their operations</li>\n<li>including: powering 10,000s of computers + powering the facility&#8217;s utilities</li>\n<li>industrial-scale energy-use is expensive</li>\n<li>engineers + policy-makers world-wide have to plan for energy needs today + tomorrow</li>\n<li>there&#8217;s a real possibility: we could run out of energy to keep-up with society&#8217;s increasing demand for data</li>\n</ul>\n<p><em>What the study discovered:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li>the study is the most detailed model to-date</li>\n<li>it looks at data centers&#8217; energy-use &#8212; plus energy efficiency gains</li>\n<li>a gain means: using energy wisely &#8212; to power more devices effectively with less energy waste</li>\n<li>engineers can improve how energy is distributed + used across the data center warehouse</li>\n<li>this lets the energy (electricity) they purchase: go farther</li>\n<li>researchers discovered that energy-use growth has been flat &#8212; over 10 years</li>\n<li>that means: engineers in data centers have been able to keep-up with energy needs + costs</li>\n<li>how: data center managers have improved the way their facilities use electricity</li>\n<li>so they&#8217;ve been able to &#8220;get the most&#8221; from energy &#8212; and not run low -or- run out of power</li>\n<li>as the data center grows &#8212; needing ever-more power &#8212; facility managers try to make energy efficiency gains</li>\n<li>at least &#8212; so far &#8212; analysts caution</li>\n<li>researchers said: &#8220;The tech industry, policy-makers, equipment-makers, facility operators can&#8217;t rest on their laurels&#8221;</li>\n<li>that means: the time will come when data center operators will not be able to keep-up</li>\n</ul>\n<p><em>What&#8217;s to come:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li>eventually, the need for more + more energy to power these facilities will grow so  large they can&#8217;t out-pace it</li>\n<li>data center operators will run out of ways to match the facility&#8217;s power needs with available electricity</li>\n<li>eventually, the availability + cost of energy will become a big problem</li>\n<li>engineers need to explore new energy tech + and new landscapes to build the biggest data centers</li>\n<li>where natural environments help with ambient cooling, or provide water + wind to harness renewable energy</li>\n<li>recent successes have been data centers built deep underground in cold, abandoned mines</li>\n<li>data centers built on lakes that cycle water to cool the facility&#8217;s computers</li>\n<li>data centers incorporating hydro-electric power</li>\n</ul>\n<p><em>The team listed steps to slow future growth in energy-use:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li>extend the life of today&#8217;s efficiency trends &#8212; strengthen standards: like <a href=\"https://www.energystar.gov\" target=\"_blank\">Energy Star</a></li>\n<li>financially reward: best energy efficiency practices</li>\n<li>financially reward: renewable energy-use to mitigate carbon emissions, in parallel</li>\n<li>invest in next-generation research &#8212; computing, storage, and heat removal tech</li>\n<li>invest in data collection, modeling, and monitoring activities &#8212; eliminate blind spots</li>\n</ul>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334588 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Northwestern Univ. - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Northwestern-Univ.-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"221\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-336787 noshadow\" title=\"photo - electric meters + wall - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-electric-meters-+-wall-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"427\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; quote &#8212;</span></p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">While the historical efficiency progress made by data centers is remarkable, our findings don&#8217;t mean IT industry and policy-makers can rest on their laurels. We think there&#8217;s enough remaining efficiency potential to last several years.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">But ever-growing demand for data means that everyone — including policy-makers, data center operators, equipment manufacturers, and data consumers — must increase efforts to avoid a sharp rise in energy-use, later this decade.</p>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">To paint a more complete picture, the research team integrated new data. Including info on data center equipment stocks, efficiency trends, and market structure. So the final model enables analysis of the energy used:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>by data center equipment &#8212; like computer servers, storage devices, and cooling systems</li>\n<li>by type of data center &#8212; including cloud and hyper-scale centers</li>\n<li>by world region</li>\n</ul>\n<p style=\"padding-left: 30px;\">The reality is we need to better monitor energy-use.</p>\n<p>&#8212; <em>Eric Masanet PhD</em></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">bio:</span> professor at Northwestern Univ.<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">bio:</span> mechanical engineer<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">bio:</span> leader: Energy + Resource Systems Analysis Lab</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; Kolos is changing the paradigm in data center infra-structure. Moving away from dense, high-cost, fossil fuel-driven areas &#8212; to an area abundant in clean, renewable energy. Beautifully integrated into the natural landscape + community, the Kolos data center will bring world-class tech industry and jobs.</p>\n<p><em>A fortress of data:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">sustainable</span> &#8212; facts &#8212;-</span><em></em></p>\n<p><em>a powerful antibiotic was discovered using an artificial intelligence software tool:</em></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">part 1:</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>researchers at MIT used intelligent software to search a library of substances for possible new antibiotics</li>\n<li>the program successfully identified a compound that has enormous promise for use as an antibiotic</li>\n<li>the antibiotic they discovered &#8212; and named &#8220;halicin&#8221; &#8212; can destroy some of the most dangerous bacteria</li>\n<li>in lab tests, the drug destroyed several of the world’s most problematic disease-causing bacteria</li>\n<li>including some strains that are resistant to all known antibiotics</li>\n<li>it also cleared infections &#8212; in 2 lab mouse tests</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">part 2:</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>the team used a software program designed for &#8220;deep learning&#8221; &#8212; a type of artificial intelligence</li>\n<li>it can see patterns in vast amounts of data &#8212; and select best-fit items that meet a researcher&#8217;s criteria</li>\n<li>the researchers showed the software how to identify types of molecules that destroy bacteria</li>\n<li>they input &#8212; into the program &#8212; a library with the molecular features of 2,500 drugs + natural compounds</li>\n<li>along with data on how well (or not) the substance blocked the growth of the bacteria named escherichia coli</li>\n<li>so the software program learned what molecular features created good antibiotics</li>\n<li>next &#8212; the team input the program with a library of 6,000 compounds</li>\n<li>these new substances were under investigation for treating various human diseases</li>\n<li>the program was set to look for compounds that had anti-microbial features</li>\n<li>but were also substantially different from current antibiotics</li>\n<li>in a few hours &#8212; the program assessed the compounds + selected some that might be good antibiotics</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">part 3:</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>the researchers used those selections to test on a range of infections</li>\n<li>the compound they named halicin &#8212; was especially effective</li>\n<li>they treated numerous drug-resistant infections with halicin</li>\n<li>halicin killed: mycobacterium tuberculosis &#8212; the bacteria that causes the serious lung illness tuberculosis</li>\n<li>halicin killed: strains of enterobacteriaceae &#8212; these bacteria are resistant to carbapenems</li>\n<li>carbapenems &#8212; are a type of antibiotic that are the last resort for enterobacteriaceae infections</li>\n<li>carbapenems &#8212; are commonly used to treat severe + high-risk bacterial infections</li>\n<li>carbapenems &#8212; are reserved for multi-drug-resistant (MDR) bacterial infections</li>\n<li>halicin cleared: the bacteria clostridiodes difficile + the bacteria acinetobacter baumannii &#8212;  in mice</li>\n<li>halicin could be a much-needed, life-saving antibiotic</li>\n<li>halicin may be able to treat the worst infections</li>\n<li>the research team is optimistic</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">part 4:</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>the World Health Organization said drug-resistant infection is one of the biggest threats to global health</li>\n<li>using artificial intelligence tech for health-care research is just beginning</li>\n<li>but major breakthroughs are already being made</li>\n</ul>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; />\n~ images<br />\n~ by definition<br />\n~ about<br />\n~ pages<br />\n~ reading<br />\n~ learning</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326670 noshadow\" title=\"photo - concrete blocks - no. 5\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-concrete-blocks-no.-5.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"426\" height=\"478\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; the story &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>Rising sea levels are quickening the pace of beach erosion around the world &#8212; endangering coastal cities + shoreline habitats. Building oyster reefs can help restore beaches and create new habitats, even as oceans rise.</p>\n<p>The living break-waters project is a new blueprint currently under construction &#8212; designed to:</p>\n<p>&#8212; control wave heights + wave power<br />\n&#8212; control dangerous shoreline erosion<br />\n&#8212; model innovation in coastal protection</p>\n<p>The special construction of the concrete blocks used in the break-water&#8217;s blueprint: includes circular indents where sea life can take root and re-build lost habitat.</p>\n<p>The living breakwaters project was crafted by the landscape architecture + design firm Scape &#8212; as part of a professional blueprint competition called Re-Build by Design, sponsored by the Dept. of Housing + Urban Development • United States.</p>\n<p>The elite competition called on top engineering firms to submit design proposals that solve major ecological, shoreline problems caused by humans + natural disasters &#8212; such as recent super-storms. Engineers explain that today&#8217;s increasing super-weather &#8212; plus the extreme use of world beaches by people &#8212; call for futuristic feats of engineering to save the shoreline&#8217;s cities + habitat.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">image</span> | above<br />\n<em>Concrete blocks called tetrapods &#8212; with an inter-locking shape &#8212; used for building modern break-waters.</em></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; the report &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">organization:</span> <a href=\"https://www.hud.gov/\" target=\"_blank\">Dept. of Housing + Urban Development</a> • United States<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">organization:</span> <a href=\"http://www.rebuildbydesign.org/\" target=\"_blank\">ReBuild by Design</a><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">report title:</span> <em>the Shallows</em><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">deck:</span> Bay Landscapes: as architectural infra-structure<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">year:</span> 2017</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">read</span> | <a href=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/FOLIO-by-ReBuild-by-Design-the-Shallows-bay-landscapes-as-ecological-infra-structure.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">the report</a><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">format:</span> <a href=\"https://acrobat.adobe.com/us/en/acrobat/pdf-reader.html\" target=\"_blank\">Adobe</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; featurette &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">group:</span> the American Museum of Natural History<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">video title:</span> the living break-waters project<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">year:</span> 2017</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">watch</span> | <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FupSGz1uuA0\" target=\"_blank\">featurette</a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FupSGz1uuA0\" target=\"_blank\"><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326200 noshadow\" title=\"everyday - play button - no. 3\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/everyday-play-button-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"140\" height=\"140\" /></a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">group:</span> Scape firm<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">video set:</span> the living break-waters project<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">year:</span> 2017</p>\n<p>The living break-waters project is an innovative, coastal green infra-structure plan &#8212; designed to reduce beach erosion + damage from storm waves, and improve the health of the delicate, shoreline eco-system.  The project also encourages the community to become good stewards of their neighborhood&#8217;s coastal zones.</p>\n<p>The project was initially developed by Scape landscape architecture + urban design firm, for the ReBuild by Design competition &#8212; held by the US Department of Housing + Urban Development to find leading-edge ideas for coastal rescue in the wake of devastating hurricanes.</p>\n<p>The project&#8217;s design is a living infra-structure that installs a necklace of break-water barriers &#8212; to buffer neighborhoods from wave damage + erosion while providing a bio-diverse habitat for juvenile fish, oysters, and more sea life.</p>\n<p>The plan is being implemented by the state of New York &#8212; with $60 million in funding. It&#8217;s currently in the schematic design process, moving into construction this year: 2019.</p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-326200 noshadow\" title=\"everyday - play button - no. 3\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/everyday-play-button-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"140\" height=\"140\" /><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">watch</span> | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/214090870\" target=\"_blank\">video</a> &#8212; no. 1<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">watch</span> | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/185561670\" target=\"_blank\">video</a> &#8212; no. 2<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">watch</span> | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/91648619\" target=\"_blank\">video</a> &#8212; no. 3</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326675 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Scape - no. 1\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Scape-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"161\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">on the web</span> | pages</p>\n<p>Scape | <a href=\"https://www.scapestudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a><br />\nScape | projects: <a href=\"https://www.scapestudio.com/projects/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a></p>\n<p>Scape | project • living break-waters &#8212; <a href=\"https://www.scapestudio.com/projects/living-breakwaters-competition/\" target=\"_blank\">part 1</a><br />\nScape | project • living break-waters &#8212; <a href=\"https://www.scapestudio.com/projects/living-breakwaters-design-implementation/\" target=\"_blank\">part 2</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326653 noshadow\" title=\"photo - concrete blocks - no. 3\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-concrete-blocks-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"373\" height=\"372\" /><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">images</span> | left + below</p>\n<p><em>These high-tech concrete blocks called tetrapods are often used in engineering modern break-waters along coastal shorelines.</em></p>\n<p><em>Concrete tetrapods were designed to remain stable under the most extreme weather + marine conditions. When they&#8217;re arranged together in lines or heaps, they create an inter-locking, porous barrier that dissipates the power of waves and currents.</em></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><a href=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/art-break-water-no.-2.png\"><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326662 noshadow\" title=\"art - break-water - no. 2\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/art-break-water-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"246\" /></a></p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-326736 noshadow\" title=\"photo - concrete blocks - no. 7\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-concrete-blocks-no.-7.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"433\" /></p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326647 noshadow\" title=\"photo - concrete blocks - no. 2\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-concrete-blocks-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"347\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">by definition</span> | tetrapods</p>\n<p>Large concrete blocks called tetrapods can be stacked side-by-side + in layers to form an inter-locking mesh &#8212; and laid-down in wide fields along shorelines to prevent erosion caused by weather and long-shore drift.</p>\n<p>Tetrapods are used by landscape engineers to re-inforce coastal structures such as seawalls and break-waters. The tetrapods have a tetrahedral shape to dissipate the force of incoming waves &#8212; this special shape helps water to flow around the blocks instead of against them. The inter-linked web they form keeps the blocks from being displaced.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">images</span> | below</p>\n<p><em>Coastal engineers survey beaches and dunes to draft blueprints for building shoreline-saving structures &#8212; like specialty overlooks for sight-seeing that don&#8217;t interfere with ecology, and break-waters made of high-concrete blocks.</em></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326638 noshadow\" title=\"photo - beach - no. 3\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-beach-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"382\" /></p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326640 noshadow\" title=\"photo - beach - no. 4\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-beach-no.-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"680\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">by definition</span> | long-shore drift</p>\n<p>Drift from long-shore current is a geological process: it means the movement of sedimentary rocks &#8212; clay, silt, sand, and shingle &#8212; along the coast, parallel to the shoreline. Incoming wind squeezes water along the coast, generating a water current that moves parallel to the coast.</p>\n<p>So long-shore drift &#8212; also called beach drift &#8212; is simply the sediment moved by the long-shore current. This current and sediment movement happen inside the surf zone.</p>\n<p>Beach sand is also moved on windy days &#8212; from the swash + back-wash of water on the beach. Breaking surf sends water up the beach (swash) &#8212; and gravity then drains the water down-slope (back-wash) perpendicular to the shoreline.</p>\n<p>Beach sand can move down the beach in a zig-zag pattern, 10s of meters per day. This causes a constant stress of erosion that takes time for nature to re-build. In cases of human-made shoreline disaster or natural storms, dangerous erosion happens much faster, threatening coastal civilization &#8212; as well as sea life + plant life habitat.</p>\n<p>The United States • Environmental Protection Agency estimates that between 80 % &#8212; 90 % of the sandy beaches along US coastlines have been eroding for decades. Many beaches are losing several inches per year. But in some cases the problem is much worse. The outer coast of the state of Louisiana &#8212; called an erosion &#8220;hot spot&#8221; &#8212; is losing 50 feet of beach per year.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326657 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - ReBuild by Design - no. 1\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-ReBuild-by-Design-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"610\" height=\"459\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">about</span> | ReBuild by Design</p>\n<p>Our cities were built in response to yesterday’s problems. The world faces rising populations, climate change, and economic challenges. So communities can’t afford to wait until after the next hurricane or flood &#8212; or ignore chronic stresses, such as aging infrastructure + pollution &#8212; to plan for the future.</p>\n<p>ReBuild by Design &#8212; a landscape architecture + urban design firm &#8212; is re-imagining the way communities find solutions for today’s large scale, complex problems. We convene a mix of sectors &#8212; government, business, non-profit, community organizations &#8212; to see how overlapping environmental + human-made vulnerabilities leave cities and regions at risk.</p>\n<p>Our core belief is: communities grow stronger with collaboration, prepared to stand-up to serious challenges. ReBuild by Design began as a design competition, launched by the United States • Dept. of Housing + Urban Development &#8212; in partnership with non-profits &#8212; in response to hurricane impact. The competition became a model to help government.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326774 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - United States - Dept. of Housing + Urban Development - no. 2\" src=\"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-United-States-Dept.-of-Housing-+-Urban-Development-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"680\" height=\"680\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">on the web</span> | pages</p>\n<p>Dept. of Housing + Urban Development • United States | <a href=\"https://www.hud.gov/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a><br />\nReBuild by Design | <a href=\"http://www.rebuildbydesign.org/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">on the web</span> | reading</p>\n<p><em>Scientific ,"http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-beach-no.-4.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn50@2020_3/2020/08/25/01-22-41-568_228211988688a944.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-ReBuild-by-Design-no.-1.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn37@2020_5/2020/08/25/01-22-27-070_707a8c41481ee36b.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-United-States-Dept.-of-Housing-+-Urban-Development-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn38@2020_1/2020/08/25/01-22-32-954_b0c09577b2d2eb43.webp","http://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-rocks-no.-1.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn49@2020_5/2020/08/25/01-22-31-527_6a526f383358953e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318532657},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","title":"Wired &#124; AI-Powered biotech can help deploy a vaccine in record time","link":"https://www.kurzweilai.net/?p=337295","description":"<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-337366 noshadow\" title=\"photo - medical + injection - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-medical-+-injection-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"466\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-313813 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Wired - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Wired-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"499\" height=\"108\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<h3><em>Wired</em> | AI-Powered biotech can help deploy a vaccine in record time</h3>\n<p><em> Simulators that can rapidly test trillions of options would accelerate the slow and costly process of human clinical trials.</em></p>\n<p><strong>by Ray Kurzweil</strong></p>\n<p>The magnitude of the Covid-19 pandemic will largely depend on how quickly safe and effective vaccines and treatments can be developed and tested. Many assume a widely available vaccine is years away, if ever. Others believe that a 12- to 18-month development cycle is a given. Our best bet to reduce even that record-breaking timeline is by using artificial intelligence.</p>\n<p>The problem is twofold: discovering the right set of molecules among billions of possibilities, and then waiting for clinical trials. These processes ordinarily take several years, but AI holds the key to radically shortening both. This is where combining AI with biotechnology is headed, and within several years all vaccine and medication development could be done this way. We can already shorten the development time of a Covid-19 vaccine using this method.</p>\n<p>Although a human trial of a vaccine or other treatment is regarded as necessary today before widespread use is approved, even large-scale trials are very imperfect, time-consuming, and expensive. A human doctor may come up with a few dozen drugs that may treat a disease. The actual number of theoretical drug possibilities is in the trillions. The current method for testing these few treatments is to organize a few hundred human subjects and then test them over about a year and a half, at a cost of hundreds of millions of dollars.</p>\n<p>Very often, the first several solutions tested on humans are not ideal and lead to other solutions that also take a few years to develop and test. We are literally stuck, watching people succumb to a disease for years while only a few possible solutions are tested. Not much can be advanced until those results are available.</p>\n<p>We are seeing the beginnings of a profound paradigm shift in health technology. AI simulations have the potential to test all of the trillions of possibilities with tens of thousands of (simulated) patients for a (simulated) period of years, and do all of this in a matter of hours or days.</p>\n<p>In 2019, for example, researchers at Flinders University in Adelaide, Australia, created a “turbocharged” flu vaccine in part by using a biology simulator that used AI to find drugs that activate the human immune system. In a matter of weeks it created trillions of chemical compounds, and the researchers used another simulator to see if each compound would be useful as an immune-boosting drug against the disease agent, selecting the ideal formulation. US researchers are now testing this optimized flu vaccine on human subjects.</p>\n<p>Moreover, in the search for antiviral drugs for Covid-19, Argonne National Laboratory has used five of the world’s most powerful supercomputers to narrow a billion molecules down to a few thousand. Then, with a combination of physics simulations to model the microscopic chemistry and deep learning for pattern recognition, they identified about 30 of the most promising candidates for laboratory study. To fight the coronavirus much more rapidly and effectively, more labs need to use AI to simulate trillions of possibilities, and then use human trials for the most promising ones.</p>\n<p>These examples mark only the beginning of AI’s contribution to overcoming health problems. Today we can simulate how small molecules interact with certain virtual or human proteins. As these methods take off in the coming years, we will be able to test all trillions of possible solutions to each health problem very quickly. Using neural nets with sufficient computational power will go way beyond what humans can possibly do on their own. Given the exponential nature of progress in this field, I believe that by the end of the decade we will be able realistically model all biology and simulate interventions for diseases without the need for human trials.</p>\n<p>Amplifying progress in creating new medications for diseases is among the most profound near-term objectives of AI. Such technology will improve medicine for a vast array of diseases, but it will also be enormously valuable when the next pandemic strikes &#8212; whenever that happens. It might have a natural origin. It might be a terrorist bioweapon. It might spread faster than Covid-19, and be 10 or 20 times as lethal. Deploying an effective cure in weeks instead of a year could save tens of millions of lives.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">about</span> | Ray Kurzweil</p>\n<p>Ray Kurzweil was the principal inventor of the CCD flat-bed scanner, omni-font optical character recognition, print-to-speech reading machine for the blind, text-to-speech synthesizer, music synthesizer capable of recreating the grand piano and other orchestral instruments, and commercially marketed large-vocabulary speech recognition.</p>\n<p>He&#8217;s received: a Grammy Award for outstanding achievements in music technology, the National Medal of Technology, 21 honorary doctorates, and is an inductee in the National Inventors Hall of Fame. Kurzweil has written 6 national best-selling books, including <em>the New York Times</em> best-seller <em>The Singularity Is Near</em> (year 2005) and <em>How To Create a Mind</em> (year 2012).</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">bio:</span> by <em>Wired</em></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; notes &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>AI = artificial intelligence<br />\nCCD = charge-coupled device</p>\n<p>COVID = corona-virus disease</p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 19 May 2020 05:00:44 +0000","feedId":11321,"bgimg":"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-medical-+-injection-no.-2.png","linkMd5":"9d78c3af6daefe9aa17cf4e08db4955a","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn70@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-22-13-490_c1d0f33c99ae9550.webp","destWidth":4000,"destHeight":2666,"sourceBytes":6450953,"destBytes":79308,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-medical-+-injection-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn70@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-22-13-490_c1d0f33c99ae9550.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Wired-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn42@2020_3/2020/08/25/01-22-27-682_9e372dcf16a1e997.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318532651},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","title":"digest &#124; above<br />\n<em>Meet Solo, the smart radio that detects your emotions + matches your moods with music.</em></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">photo:</span> by Uniform</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; in this post &#8211;</span></p>\n<p>~ featurette<br />\n~ story<br />\n~ reading</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-332053 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Uniform - no. 4\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Uniform-no.-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"116\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-326200 noshadow\" title=\"everyday - play button - no. 3\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/everyday-play-button-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"140\" height=\"140\" /><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; featurette &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">group:</span> Uniform<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">featurette title:</span> Solo: the emotional radio</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">watch</span> | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/297026707\" target=\"_blank\">featurette</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; story &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>Solo is a smart digital radio that interacts with people &#8212; scanning the faces on on-lookers to determine their moods, then finding the perfect song to match how you feel.</p>\n<p>Built by the innovative product design studio Uniform, Solo explores the shift towards a more human artificial intelligence. Uniform calls Solo an &#8220;emotional radio&#8221; &#8212; that heralds the future of friendlier, more playful computer software. The concept project is deepening our human + machine interaction.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">How it works.<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Solo combines facial feature recognition with music valence &#8212; to read nuances of expression and match songs to your current mood.</p>\n<p>Sensing movement, Solo draws you in with its artsy antenna. As you get closer, it takes your photo. Then Solo sends that photo to a Microsoft application program interface &#8212; that analyses facial features &#8212; and sends that info back again as an emotional breakdown, with values measuring your happiness, sadness, and upset.</p>\n<p>Solo translates these figures into an emotional valence rating that corresponds with Spotify’s track emotional valence ratings. Then Solo plays the song it thinks you want to hear most. Kind of like a mix CD from a friend who knows you personally.</p>\n<p>Solo highlights an AI capability called atypical feature recognition. The designers at Uniform predict this skill will improve &#8212; as computer software algorithms become more sophisticated.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">What is emotional valence?<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>Psychologists use the phrase emotional valence to describe whether something is likely to make you feel happy (positive valence) or sad (negative valence). Is an event, situation, or experience going to add positivity to your mood &#8212; or take-away from it? That’s how you can determine something&#8217;s emotional valence.</p>\n<p>People&#8217;s reaction to music is emotional. Some of it makes us happy, and some of it makes us sad &#8212; with songs falling along the spectrum between positive -to- negative.</p>\n<p>At Spotify &#8212; the music service &#8212; the engineers index the songs according to their emotional valence. They decide the valence based on a wide range of inputs in a general framework of what positive music sounds like.</p>\n<ul>\n<li>high valence • positive = happy • cheerful • euphoric • excited</li>\n<li>low valence • negative = sad • depressed • frustrated • angry</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">Connecting with humans.<br />\n</span></p>\n<p>AI has much to learn about our aesthetic individuality, and Solo explores a more sensitive human + machine connection through the medium of music. Uniform created Solo to showcase how AI can be programmed with empathy.</p>\n<p>The future of software + device design will go beyond data / services &#8212; toward better human interaction. This especially has implications for service robots in household, health care, and hospitality. And for personal assistants that live on smart-phones + smart-home appliances.</p>\n<p>The engineers at Uniform said: &#8220;When you try Solo, you think about how tech is changing &#8212; and how its relationship with us is changing. So as computer intelligence goes deeper into our daily life, it must understand us emotionally. And engage us in more human ways.&#8221;</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"wp-image-332013 noshadow alignleft\" title=\"photo - wood figures w. moods - no. 1\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-wood-figures-w.-moods-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"418\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">image</span> | above</p>\n<p>The Solo prototype uses facial recognition &#8212; an artificial intelligence tech &#8212; to scan human faces from photographs and make a visual map of different expressions. Each type of physical face expression is categorized by the team &#8212; and labeled with a mood: angry, happy, sad, thoughtful, scared, excited.</p>\n<p>When Solo takes a person&#8217;s facial photo, the artificial intelligence engine can make a pattern match to the expressions indexed in the team&#8217;s database &#8212; and assign the face&#8217;s mood to any new photo it takes, using this look-up table.</p>\n<p>In the next step, Solo matches the mood it&#8217;s assigned to a face photo to a song that is tagged on Spotify with the same mood. So a facial photo that is labeled &#8220;sad&#8221; will play a matching &#8220;sad&#8221; song. When a &#8220;happy&#8221; human face is detected, Solo will play a &#8220;happy&#8221; song.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"size-full wp-image-332000 noshadow alignleft\" title=\"story - brand - Uniform - no. 3\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Uniform-no.-3.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"324\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ff9900;\">on the web</span> | pages</p>\n<p>Uniform | <a href=\"http://uniform.net/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a><br />\nUniform | <a href=\"http://uniform.net/work/projects/solo/\" target=\"_blank\">Solo</a></p>\n<p>Uniform | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/uniformltd\" target=\"_blank\">Vimeo channel</a><br />\nUniform | <a href=\"https://vimeo.com/297026718\" target=\"_blank\">featurette</a>: studio profile</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ff9900;\">on the web</span> | pages</p>\n<p>Microsoft | <a href=\"https://www.microsoft.com/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a><br />\nSpotify | <a href=\"https://www.spotify.com/\" target=\"_blank\">home</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\" wp-image-332074 noshadow alignleft\" title=\"story - brand - Spotify - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Spotify-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"233\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; a &#38; e</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">[ end of file ]</span></p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 25 Oct 2019 05:00:44 +0000","feedId":11321,"bgimg":"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-Solo-smart-radio-no.-2.png","linkMd5":"4a9d63397859e9353bc3c7028e43809b","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn1@2020_2/2020/08/25/01-22-15-597_5827e85ff9a920ce.webp","destWidth":3840,"destHeight":2483,"sourceBytes":4793219,"destBytes":230004,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-Solo-smart-radio-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn1@2020_2/2020/08/25/01-22-15-597_5827e85ff9a920ce.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Uniform-no.-4.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn67@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-33-718_248330f49f7fee46.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/everyday-play-button-no.-3.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn28@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-30-567_f72f234d72f63e13.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-wood-figures-w.-moods-no.-1.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn80@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-22-32-720_48b34417b540c7ed.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Uniform-no.-3.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn44@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-22-35-411_7f313493a368312d.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Spotify-no.-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn88@2020_2/2020/08/25/01-22-34-195_2f8b496265e72813.webp","https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/everyday-newspaper-no.-21.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn0@2020_1/404.jpg"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318532656},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:22:12","title":"digest &#124; A connection between digital lifestyle + depression","link":"http://www.kurzweilai.net/?p=256758","description":"<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-335272 noshadow\" title=\"photo - form + health-care - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-form-+-health-care-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"1048\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><iframe id=\"speechkit-io-iframe\" style=\"display: none;\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"240\" scrolling=\"no\" width=\"320\" data-src=\"https://spkt.io/a/446143\"></iframe><br />\n<script type=\"text/javascript\" src=\"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@speechkit/speechkit-audio-player@latest/dist/speechkit-iframe-helper.js\"></script></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; in this post &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>~ story<br />\n~ chart<br />\n~ by the numbers<br />\n~ pages<br />\n~ reading</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; story &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>Researchers at Northwestern Univ. believe a smart-phone app they developed called Purple Robot can detect depression in people by tracking:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>the number of daily minutes you use a mobile phone</li>\n<li>plus your daily geographic location pattern</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Using this smart-phone data collection app, the researchers correlated that the more time a person spends using a mobile phone, the more likely they&#8217;re depressed. The average daily mobile phone use for depressed people was 68 minutes &#8212; and for non-depressed people it was 17 minutes.</p>\n<p>Another pattern researchers noticed was related to a person&#8217;s location. Spending most of their time at home, and most of their time in fewer locations &#8212; as measured by GPS tracking on their mobile phone &#8212; was linked to depression. Also linked to depression: having a less regular day-to-day schedule, and going to work at different times each day.</p>\n<p>The study resulted in a significant outcome: the researchers were able to predict if somebody was depressed &#8212; just by looking at this mobile phone data &#8212; with 87% accuracy.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">The research study.</span></p>\n<p>28 adult participants were recruited from the community to carry a mobile phone with the sensor data acquisition app &#8212; called Purple Robot &#8212; for 2 weeks. Before the 2-weeks started: to determine if they were depressed, the participants filled-out a standard questionnaire that measures the signs + symptoms of depression.</p>\n<p>The questionnaire is called PHQ-9 &#8212; it&#8217;s widely used by health-care providers, and relies on the patient self-reporting their feelings + experiences. The form asks about common symptoms used to diagnose depression &#8212; on a scale of 1 -to- 10.</p>\n<p>symptoms used to diagnose depression:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>sadness</li>\n<li>hopelessness</li>\n<li>loss of pleasure</li>\n<li>loss of appetite</li>\n<li>difficulty sleeping</li>\n<li>difficulty concentrating</li>\n</ul>\n<p>according to the PHQ-9 questionnaire:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>14 participants did not have signs of depression</li>\n<li>14 had symptoms of depression &#8212; ranging from mild -to- severe</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Researchers analyzed the GPS locations and phone use for the 28 individuals &#8212; 20 females + 8 males, average age of 29 years-old &#8212; for 2 weeks. The sensor tracked GPS location every 5 minutes.</p>\n<p>Then &#8212; using the GPS + phone use data collected from the mobile phones &#8212; the researchers correlated those results with the participants&#8217; depression test results. They were able to see a pattern emerge, accurately matching the trends in the data with people who self-reported as depressed or not depressed.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-335268 noshadow\" title=\"photo - guy + mobile phone - no. 7\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-guy-+-mobile-phone-no.-7.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"393\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p>MAP</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-334566 noshadow\" title=\"photo - girl + mobile phone - no. 6\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-girl-+-mobile-phone-no.-6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"466\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">chart</span> | below</p>\n<ul>\n<li>A chart from the study showing an example of mobile phone use data from 1 participant.</li>\n<li>Each column is a day of the week during the 2 week study.</li>\n<li>The grey bars show the amount of time during the day the particpant&#8217;s smart-phone was active.</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">art:</span> by Center for Behavioral Intervention Technologies • Northwestern Univ.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; chart &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-335128 noshadow\" title=\"art - chart + mobile for depression - no. 6\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/art-chart-+-mobile-for-depression-no.-6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"1044\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">Signs of depression surfacing.</span></p>\n<p>David Mohr PhD is a clinical psychologist &#8212; and Director of the Center for Behavioral Intervention Technologies at Northwestern Univ.</p>\n<p>He said: &#8220;The significance of this research is we can detect if somebody has depression &#8212; and the severity of their symptoms &#8212; without asking them any questions. We&#8217;re detecting depression with smart-phones &#8212; that are providing data passively.</p>\n<p>&#8220;The research data showed that depressed people don&#8217;t usually go to many places &#8212; that reflects the loss of motivation seen with depression. So depressed people withdraw. They don’t have the motivation or energy to go out and do things.”</p>\n<p>Depression is a mental health disorder that&#8217;s common, upsetting, and often recurring. It frequently goes un-detected + un-treated. Today&#8217;s mobile phones are everywhere &#8212; and have a large complement of sensors that can monitor the behavior patterns of their users. Those patterns might be a key to discovering symptoms of depression.</p>\n<p>The mobile phone use data didn’t identify how people were using their phones. But Mohr suspects that people who spent the most time on their smart-phones were surfing the web or playing games &#8212; probably not talking with friends.</p>\n<p>He said: “When people are on their smart-phones, they&#8217;re likely to avoid thinking about painful things, or difficult relationships. It’s an avoidance behavior that&#8217;s common with depression.”</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">Better than questionnaires.</span></p>\n<p>The smart-phone data was better at detecting depression than daily questions the participants answered about how sad they were feeling on a scale of 1 -to- 10. Those answers are often un-reliable.</p>\n<p>This research can develop new ways of monitoring people at risk for depression &#8212; and enable health care providers to intervene more quickly. If the app watching the mobile phone detects patterns of activity associated with depression &#8212; an alert can be sent to physicians to get people the care they need.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">Future studies + conclusions.</span></p>\n<p>Next, the researchers plan to study: if getting people to change the behaviors linked to depression can improve their mood.</p>\n<p>Mohr said: “We&#8217;ll see if we can reduce symptoms of depression by encouraging people to: maintain a more regular routine, spend more time in a variety of places, and reduce their mobile phone use.&#8221;</p>\n<p>In conclusion, mobile phone sensors offer clinical opportunities:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>provide continuous monitoring of at-risk people</li>\n<li>with little burden on the patient to recognize or diagnose their own symptoms</li>\n<li>provide a calming sense of medical supervision to people suffering with depression</li>\n<li>provide just-in-time outreach + interventions</li>\n</ul>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334693 noshadow\" title=\"photo - hands + desktop tools - no. 6\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-hands-+-desktop-tools-no.-6.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"291\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334840 noshadow\" title=\"photo - form + health-care - no. 4\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-form-+-health-care-no.-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"534\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; by the numbers &#8212;</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>depression is a serious medical condition</li>\n<li>it is life-affecting + can be life-threatening</li>\n<li>symptoms include: sadness, loss of pleasure, low energy, difficulty concentrating, and suicidal thoughts</li>\n<li>depression affects 20 million people in the US</li>\n<li>depression affects 300 million people world-wide</li>\n<li>depression is the single biggest cause of disability world-wide</li>\n<li></li>\n<li>it affects every age, ethnicity, gender, religion, culture, and economic community</li>\n<li>the class of prescription drugs called anti-depressants are only 50% effective in treating its symptoms</li>\n<li>there haven&#8217;t been any new treatments for depression on the horizon for +20 years</li>\n<li>depression research is under-funded</li>\n<li>we need better treatments for + understanding of this illness</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">source:</span> <a href=\"https://www.hopefordepression.org/depression-facts\" target=\"_blank\">Hope for Depression Research Foundation</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft size-full wp-image-334895 noshadow\" title=\"photo - umbrella + open - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-umbrella-+-open-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"466\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; types of depression &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>The umbrella of depressive illness:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>major depression disorder</li>\n<li>persistent depression disorder</li>\n<li>mood disorder</li>\n<li>anxiety disorder</li>\n<li>seasonal depression disorder</li>\n<li>menstrual cycle depression disorder</li>\n<li>pregnancy depression disorder</li>\n<li>post-traumatic loss depression disorder</li>\n<li>post-traumatic stress depression disorder</li>\n<li>thoughts of suicide</li>\n</ul>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; signals of depression &#8212;</span></p>\n<ul>\n<li>feelings: sad, worthless, guilty</li>\n<li>missing: school, job, appointments</li>\n<li>activities: lack of pleasure or interest</li>\n<li>big changes: in appetite or weight</li>\n<li>sluggishness + lethargy</li>\n<li>withdrawing from: friends + family</li>\n<li>new behaviors like: restlessness, fits, fidgeting</li>\n<li>difficulty: falling asleep or staying asleep</li>\n<li>difficulty: organizing, concentrating, remembering</li>\n<li>self-harming: thoughts + actions</li>\n</ul>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">source:</span> <a href=\"https://www.hopefordepression.org/depression-facts\" target=\"_blank\">Hope for Depression Research Foundation</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\"><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334700 noshadow\" title=\"photo - girl + laptop - no. 4\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/photo-girl-+-laptop-no.-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"538\" /></span></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334759 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Pfizer - no. 1\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Pfizer-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"216\" height=\"127\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; questionnaire &#8212;</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">group:</span> by <a href=\"http://www.Pfizer.com\" target=\"_blank\">Pfizer</a><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">form:</span> Patient Health Questionnaire 9<br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">for:</span> diagnosing depression</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">read</span> | <a href=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/FOLIO-by-Pfizer-Patient-Health-Questionnaire-9.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">questionnaire</a><br />\n<span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">format:</span> <a href=\"https://acrobat.adobe.com/us/en/acrobat/pdf-reader.html\" target=\"_blank\">Adobe</a></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">about</span> | questionnaire</p>\n<p>The form called Patient Health Questionnaire 9 (PHQ-9) &#8212; developed by pharmaceutical company Pfizer &#8212; is an important medical standard for diagnosing depression.</p>\n<p>Patients fill-out the 9 question form &#8212; it takes just 5 minutes. They answer questions about symptoms + feelings they experience. The questionnaire gives physicians a good basis for discovering depression in patients who may not know how or why they&#8217;re suffering.</p>\n<p>The form is a mainstay of health-care providers &#8212; but researchers are looking for better ways to detect depression without asking patients to self-describe their symptoms. Because that technique can be un-reliable. If depression goes un-detected, symptoms can increase and people don&#8217;t get the help they need to cope.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334588 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Northwestern Univ. - no. 2\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Northwestern-Univ.-no.-2.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"221\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334586 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Northwestern Univ. - no. 1\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Northwestern-Univ.-no.-1.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"486\" height=\"486\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-334591 noshadow\" title=\"story - brand - Center for Behavioral InterventionTechnologies - Northwestern Univ. - no. 4\" src=\"https://www.kurzweilai.net/images/story-brand-Center-for-Behavioral-InterventionTechnologies-Northwestern-Univ.-no.-4.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"700\" height=\"181\" /></p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">on the web</span> | pages</p>\n<p>Center for Behavioral Intervention Technologies • Northwestern Univ. | <a href=\"http://cbits.northwestern.edu\" target=\"_blank\">home</a><br />\nCenter for Behavioral Intervention Technologies • Northwestern Univ. | <a href=\"https://tech.cbits.northwestern.edu/purple-robot\" target=\"_blank\">Purple Robot</a></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">tag line:</span> Envisioning a world with effective, usable, and sustainable digital mental health services for all people.</p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">motto:</span> Whatsoever things are true.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">&#8212; summary &#8212;</span></p>\n<p>At the center, we evaluate behavioral intervention tech-enabled services. We explore new techniques for mental health and well-being &#8212; that are proven scientifically effective.</p>\n<p>We analyze data from smart-phone sensors. An ever-increasing amount + variety of sensors are collecting and transmitting data about our lives. This data is used by companies for advertising &#8212; but can also help us with daily tasks. For example: sensor data from our mobile phones is collected to see best driving routes that avoid traffic. And step-counting sensors track walking fitness.</p>\n<p>We&#8217;re learning how sensor data can improve life for people with mental health issues. Our &#8220;personal sensing&#8221; research harnesses sensor data collected from mobile devices &#8212; to identify behaviors + states associated with mental health. Then patterns are identified to improve digital mental health interventions like apps + bots.</p>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><span style=\"color: #ffaa00;\">about</span> | Purple Robot</p>\n<p>The Purple Robot app &#8212; built for the Android mobile operating system owned by Google &#8212; provides a real-time sensor data platform for collecting info about the smart-phone user, and their surroundings.</p>\n<p><em>Purple Robot provides:</em></p>\n<ul>\n<li>access to the Android operating system&#8217;s sensor framework</li>\n<li>including: accelerometer, gyroscope, pressure sensor</li>\n<li>access to other device info: battery level, running software + apps, and hardware</li>\n<li>options to scan for external devices like: wireless access points + visible BlueTooth devices</li>\n<li>location sensors that use: the built-in GPS + cellular triangulation to map user location</li>\n<li>local environment like: solar event timing (sunrise + sunset) and weather</li>\n<li>statistical summary of the user’s communication pattern</li>\n<li>including: phone logs + text-message transcripts</li>\n<li>cryptographic anonymization of personal identity info before it leaves the device</li>\n</ul>\n<hr class=\"dotted\" />\n<p><img style=' float: left; padding: 4px; margin: 0 7px 2px 0;'  class=\"alignleft  wp-image-335678 noshadow\" title=\"photo -
